Utah Code Annotated - Title 17B - Limited Purpose Local Government Entities - Special Districts
===============================================================================================

Utah Code Annotated - Title 17B - Chapter 1 - Provisions Applicable to All Special Districts
********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this title:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(1): "Appointing authority" means the person or body authorized to make an appointment to the board of trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(2): "Basic special district":
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(2)(a): means a special district that is not a specialized special district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(2)(b): includes an entity that was, under the law in effect before April 30, 2007, created and operated as a special district, as defined under the law in effect before April 30, 2007.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(3): Title 11, Chapter 14, Local Government Bonding Act; Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act "Bond" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(3)(a): a written obligation to repay borrowed money, whether denominated a bond, note, warrant, certificate of indebtedness, or otherwise; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(3)(b): Title 11, Chapter 14, Local Government Bonding Act; Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act a lease agreement, installment purchase agreement, or other agreement that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(3)(b)(i): includes an obligation by the district to pay money; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(3)(b)(ii): Title 11, Chapter 14, Local Government Bonding Act; Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act the district's board of trustees, in its discretion, treats as a bond for purposes of
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(4): Chapter 2a, Part 1, Cemetery Maintenance District Act "Cemetery maintenance district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(5): Chapter 2a, Part 2, Drainage District Act "Drainage district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(6): "Facility" or "facilities" includes any structure, building, system, land, water right, water, or other real or personal property required to provide a service that a special district is authorized to provide, including any related or appurtenant easement or right-of-way, improvement, utility, landscaping, sidewalk, road, curb, gutter, equipment, or furnishing.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(7): Chapter 2a, Part 3, Fire Protection District Act "Fire protection district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8): "General obligation bond":
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(a): means a bond that is directly payable from and secured by ad valorem property taxes that are:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(a)(i): levied:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(a)(i)(A): by the district that issues the bond; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(a)(i)(B): on taxable property within the district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(a)(ii): in excess of the ad valorem property taxes of the district for the current fiscal year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(b): does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(b)(i): a short-term bond;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(b)(ii): a tax and revenue anticipation bond; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(8)(b)(iii): a special assessment bond.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(9): "Improvement assurance" means a surety bond, letter of credit, cash, or other security:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(9)(a): to guarantee the proper completion of an improvement;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(9)(b): that is required before a special district may provide a service requested by a service applicant; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(9)(c): that is offered to a special district to induce the special district before construction of an improvement begins to:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(9)(c)(i): provide the requested service; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(9)(c)(ii): commit to provide the requested service.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(10): "Improvement assurance warranty" means a promise that the materials and workmanship of an improvement:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(10)(a): comply with standards adopted by a special district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(10)(b): will not fail in any material respect within an agreed warranty period.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(11): Chapter 2a, Part 4, Improvement District Act "Improvement district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(12): Chapter 2a, Part 5, Irrigation District Act "Irrigation district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(13): Chapter 2a, Part 6, Metropolitan Water District Act "Metropolitan water district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(14): Chapter 2a, Part 7, Mosquito Abatement District Act "Mosquito abatement district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(15): "Municipal" means of or relating to a municipality.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(16): "Municipality" means a city, town, or metro township.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(17): Chapter 2a, Part 11, Municipal Services District Act "Municipal services district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(18): "Person" means an individual, corporation, partnership, organization, association, trust, governmental agency, or other legal entity.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(19): Title 17D, Chapter 1, Special Service District Act; Title 11, Chapter 13, Interlocal Cooperation Act "Political subdivision" means a county, city, town, metro township, special district under this title, special service district under
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(20): "Private," with respect to real property, means not owned by the United States or any agency of the federal government, the state, a county, or a political subdivision.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(21): "Public entity" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(21)(a): the United States or an agency of the United States;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(21)(b): the state or an agency of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(21)(c): a political subdivision of the state or an agency of a political subdivision of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(21)(d): another state or an agency of that state; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(21)(e): a political subdivision of another state or an agency of that political subdivision.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(22): Chapter 2a, Part 8, Public Transit District Act "Public transit district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(23): "Revenue bond":
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(23)(a): means a bond payable from designated taxes or other revenues other than the special district's ad valorem property taxes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(23)(b): does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(23)(b)(i): an obligation constituting an indebtedness within the meaning of an applicable constitutional or statutory debt limit;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(23)(b)(ii): a tax and revenue anticipation bond; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(23)(b)(iii): a special assessment bond.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(24): "Rules of order and procedure" means a set of rules that govern and prescribe in a public meeting:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(24)(a): parliamentary order and procedure;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(24)(b): ethical behavior; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(24)(c): civil discourse.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(25): "Service applicant" means a person who requests that a special district provide a service that the special district is authorized to provide.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(26): Chapter 2a, Part 9, Service Area Act "Service area" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(27): "Short-term bond" means a bond that is required to be repaid during the fiscal year in which the bond is issued.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(28): "Special assessment" means an assessment levied against property to pay all or a portion of the costs of making improvements that benefit the property.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(29): "Special assessment bond" means a bond payable from special assessments.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30): 17B-1-103; Chapter 2a, Part 1, Cemetery Maintenance District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 2, Drainage District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 3, Fire Protection District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 4, Improvement District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 5, Irrigation District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 6, Metropolitan Water District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 7, Mosquito Abatement District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 8, Public Transit District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 9, Service Area Act; Chapter 2a, Part 10, Water Conservancy District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 11, Municipal Services District Act "Special district" means a limited purpose local government entity, as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(a): this chapter; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b): Chapter 2a, Part 1, Cemetery Maintenance District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 2, Drainage District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 3, Fire Protection District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 4, Improvement District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 5, Irrigation District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 6, Metropolitan Water District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 7, Mosquito Abatement District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 8, Public Transit District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 9, Service Area Act; Chapter 2a, Part 10, Water Conservancy District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 11, Municipal Services District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(i): this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii): Chapter 2a, Part 1, Cemetery Maintenance District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 2, Drainage District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 3, Fire Protection District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 4, Improvement District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 5, Irrigation District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 6, Metropolitan Water District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 7, Mosquito Abatement District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 8, Public Transit District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 9, Service Area Act; Chapter 2a, Part 10, Water Conservancy District Act; Chapter 2a, Part 11, Municipal Services District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(A): Chapter 2a, Part 1, Cemetery Maintenance District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(B): Chapter 2a, Part 2, Drainage District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(C): Chapter 2a, Part 3, Fire Protection District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(D): Chapter 2a, Part 4, Improvement District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(E): Chapter 2a, Part 5, Irrigation District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(F): Chapter 2a, Part 6, Metropolitan Water District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(G): Chapter 2a, Part 7, Mosquito Abatement District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(H): Chapter 2a, Part 8, Public Transit District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(I): Chapter 2a, Part 9, Service Area Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(J): Chapter 2a, Part 10, Water Conservancy District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(30)(b)(ii)(K): Chapter 2a, Part 11, Municipal Services District Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(31): "Specialized special district" means a special district that is a cemetery maintenance district, a drainage district, a fire protection district, an improvement district, an irrigation district, a metropolitan water district, a mosquito abatement district, a public transit district, a service area, a water conservancy district, a municipal services district, or a public infrastructure district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(32): "Taxable value" means the taxable value of property as computed from the most recent equalized assessment roll for county purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(33): "Tax and revenue anticipation bond" means a bond:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(33)(a): issued in anticipation of the collection of taxes or other revenues or a combination of taxes and other revenues; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(33)(b): that matures within the same fiscal year as the fiscal year in which the bond is issued.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(34): "Unincorporated" means not included within a municipality.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(35): Chapter 2a, Part 10, Water Conservancy District Act "Water conservancy district" means a special district that operates under and is subject to the provisions of this chapter and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-102(36): "Works" includes a dam, reservoir, well, canal, conduit, pipeline, drain, tunnel, power plant, and any facility, improvement, or property necessary or convenient for supplying or treating water for any beneficial use, and for otherwise accomplishing the purposes of a special district.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103 Special district status and powers -- Registration as a limited purpose entity.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(1): A special district:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(1)(a): is:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(1)(a)(i): a body corporate and politic with perpetual succession;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(1)(a)(ii): a quasi-municipal corporation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(1)(a)(iii): a political subdivision of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(1)(b): may sue and be sued.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2): (2)(a); (b); Part 11, Special District Bonds; Part 10, Special District Property Tax Levy; Title 78B, Chapter 6, Part 5, Eminent Domain; Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act; (3); 53C-1-103; 53C-1-102; 53C-1-303; 73-3-29; (2)(r)(ii); Title 11, Chapter 42, Assessment Area Act; 17B-1-202(1); Title 11, Chapter 42, Assessment Area Act A special district may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(a): acquire, by any lawful means, or lease any real property, personal property, or a groundwater right necessary or convenient to the full exercise of the district's powers;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(b): acquire, by any lawful means, any interest in real property, personal property, or a groundwater right necessary or convenient to the full exercise of the district's powers;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(c): (2)(a); (b) transfer an interest in or dispose of any property or interest described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(d): acquire or construct works, facilities, and improvements necessary or convenient to the full exercise of the district's powers, and operate, control, maintain, and use those works, facilities, and improvements;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(e): borrow money and incur indebtedness for any lawful district purpose;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(f): Part 11, Special District Bonds issue bonds, including refunding bonds:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(f)(i): for any lawful district purpose; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(f)(ii): Part 11, Special District Bonds as provided in and subject to
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(g): Part 10, Special District Property Tax Levy levy and collect property taxes:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(g)(i): for any lawful district purpose or expenditure, including to cover a deficit resulting from tax delinquencies in a preceding year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(g)(ii): Part 10, Special District Property Tax Levy as provided in and subject to
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(h): Title 78B, Chapter 6, Part 5, Eminent Domain as provided in
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(i): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act invest money as provided in
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j)(i): impose fees or other charges for commodities, services, or facilities provided by the district, to pay some or all of the district's costs of providing the commodities, services, and facilities, including the costs of:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j)(i)(A): maintaining and operating the district;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j)(i)(B): acquiring, purchasing, constructing, improving, or enlarging district facilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j)(i)(C): issuing bonds and paying debt service on district bonds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j)(i)(D): providing a reserve established by the board of trustees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(j)(ii): take action the board of trustees considers appropriate and adopt regulations to assure the collection of all fees and charges that the district imposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(k): if applicable, charge and collect a fee to pay for the cost of connecting a customer's property to district facilities in order for the district to provide service to the property;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(l): enter into a contract that the special district board of trustees considers necessary, convenient, or desirable to carry out the district's purposes, including a contract:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(l)(i): with the United States or any department or agency of the United States;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(l)(ii): to indemnify and save harmless; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(l)(iii): to do any act to exercise district powers;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(m): purchase supplies, equipment, and materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(n): encumber district property upon terms and conditions that the board of trustees considers appropriate;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(o): exercise other powers and perform other functions that are provided by law;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(p): (3); 53C-1-103; 53C-1-102; 53C-1-303; 73-3-29 construct and maintain works and establish and maintain facilities, including works or facilities:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(p)(i): (3) across or along any public street or highway, subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(p)(i)(A): promptly restores the street or highway, as much as practicable, to its former state of usefulness; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(p)(i)(B): does not use the street or highway in a manner that completely or unnecessarily impairs the usefulness of it;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(p)(ii): 53C-1-103; 53C-1-102; 53C-1-303 in, upon, or over any vacant public lands that are or become the property of the state, including school and institutional trust lands, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(p)(iii): 73-3-29 across any stream of water or watercourse, subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(q): perform any act or exercise any power reasonably necessary for the efficient operation of the special district in carrying out its purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(r): (2)(r)(ii); Title 11, Chapter 42, Assessment Area Act; 17B-1-202(1); Title 11, Chapter 42, Assessment Area Act
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(r)(i): (2)(r)(ii); Title 11, Chapter 42, Assessment Area Act except for a special district described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(r)(ii): 17B-1-202(1); Title 11, Chapter 42, Assessment Area Act for a special district created to assess a groundwater right in a critical management area described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(s): contract with another political subdivision of the state to allow the other political subdivision to use the district's surplus water or capacity or have an ownership interest in the district's works or facilities, upon the terms and for the consideration, whether monetary or nonmonetary consideration or no consideration, that the district's board of trustees considers to be in the best interests of the district and the public;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t): upon the terms and for the consideration, whether monetary or nonmonetary consideration or no consideration, that the district's board of trustees considers to be in the best interests of the district and the public, agree:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t)(i): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t)(i)(A): with another political subdivision of the state; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t)(i)(B): with a public or private owner of property on which the district has a right-of-way or adjacent to which the district owns fee title to property; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t)(ii): to allow the use of property:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t)(ii)(A): owned by the district; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(t)(ii)(B): on which the district has a right-of-way; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(u): if the special district receives, as determined by the special district board of trustees, adequate monetary or nonmonetary consideration in return:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(u)(i): provide services or nonmonetary assistance to a nonprofit entity;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(u)(ii): waive fees required to be paid by a nonprofit entity; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(2)(u)(iii): provide monetary assistance to a nonprofit entity, whether from the special district's own funds or from funds the special district receives from the state or any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3): (2)(p)(i) With respect to a special district's use of a street or highway, as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(a): the district shall comply with the reasonable rules and regulations of the governmental entity, whether state, county, or municipal, with jurisdiction over the street or highway, concerning:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(a)(i): an excavation and the refilling of an excavation;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(a)(ii): the relaying of pavement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(a)(iii): the protection of the public during a construction period; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(b): the governmental entity, whether state, county, or municipal, with jurisdiction over the street or highway:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(b)(i): may not require the district to pay a license or permit fee or file a bond; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(3)(b)(ii): may require the district to pay a reasonable inspection fee.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4): (4)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a): (4)(b) A special district may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(i): acquire, lease, or construct and operate electrical generation, transmission, and distribution facilities, if:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(i)(A): the purpose of the facilities is to harness energy that results inherently from the district's operation of a project or facilities that the district is authorized to operate or from the district providing a service that the district is authorized to provide;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(i)(B): the generation of electricity from the facilities is incidental to the primary operations of the district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(i)(C): operation of the facilities will not hinder or interfere with the primary operations of the district;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(ii): (4)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(ii)(A): use electricity generated by the facilities; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(a)(ii)(B): (4)(b) subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(b): A district may not act as a retail distributor or seller of electricity.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(4)(c): Revenue that a district receives from the sale of electricity from electrical generation facilities it owns or operates under this section may be used for any lawful district purpose, including the payment of bonds issued to pay some or all of the cost of acquiring or constructing the facilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(5): A special district may adopt and, after adoption, alter a corporate seal.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(6): 67-1a-15; (6)(a); 67-1a-15; 67-3-1
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(6)(a): 67-1a-15 Each special district shall register and maintain the special district's registration as a limited purpose entity, in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(6)(b): (6)(a); 67-1a-15; 67-3-1 A special district that fails to comply with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(7): (7)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(7)(a): (7) As used in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(7)(b): The authority to regulate a knife is reserved to the state except where the Legislature specifically delegates responsibility to a special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-103(7)(c): Unless specifically authorized by the Legislature by statute, a special district may not adopt or enforce a regulation or rule pertaining to a knife.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104 Property owner provisions.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1): (1)(a)(ii); Part 4, Annexation; 63H-1-102; Title 63H, Chapter 1, Military Installation Development Authority Act; Title 59, Chapter 2, Part 3, County Assessment; Title 59, Chapter 2, Part 2, Assessment of Property For purposes of this title:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(a): (1)(a)(ii); Part 4, Annexation; 63H-1-102; Title 63H, Chapter 1, Military Installation Development Authority Act the owner of real property shall be:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(a)(i): (1)(a)(ii) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(a)(ii): Part 4, Annexation; 63H-1-102; Title 63H, Chapter 1, Military Installation Development Authority Act for a proposed annexation under
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(b): Title 59, Chapter 2, Part 3, County Assessment; Title 59, Chapter 2, Part 2, Assessment of Property the value of private real property shall be determined according to the last assessment before the filing of the request or petition, as determined by:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(b)(i): Title 59, Chapter 2, Part 3, County Assessment the county under
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(b)(ii): Title 59, Chapter 2, Part 2, Assessment of Property the State Tax Commission under
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(1)(b)(iii): the county, for all other property.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(2): (2)(a)(ii); (2)(b) For purposes of each provision of this title that requires the owners of private real property covering a percentage of the total private land area within the proposed special district to sign a request, petition, or protest:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(2)(a): (2)(a)(ii) a parcel of real property may not be included in the calculation of the required percentage unless the request or petition is signed by:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(2)(a)(i): (2)(a)(ii) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-104(2)(a)(ii): if the parcel is owned by joint tenants or tenants by the entirety, 50% of the number of owners of that parcel;

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-113 Liability insurance.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-113(1): Each special district with an annual operating budget of $50,000 or more shall obtain liability insurance as considered appropriate by the special district board.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-113(2): Each special district with an annual operating budget of less than $50,000 is not required to obtain liability insurance, but liability insurance is encouraged, as considered appropriate by the special district board.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-114 Special district property taxes on a parity with general taxes.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Unless otherwise specifically provided by statute, property taxes levied by a special district shall constitute a lien on the property on a parity with and collectible at the same time and in the same manner as general county taxes that are a lien on the property.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-115 Validation of previously created special districts -- Continuation of certain special districts under this chapter -- Providing a previously authorized service.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-115(1): Each special district created before April 30, 2007 under the law in effect at the time of the creation is declared to be validly and legally constituted.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-115(2): Chapter 2a, Provisions Applicable to Different Types of Special Districts An entity created and operating under the law in effect before April 30, 2007 as a special district but not as a cemetery maintenance district, drainage district, fire protection district, improvement district, irrigation district, metropolitan water district, mosquito abatement district, public transit district, service area, or water conservancy district shall continue on and after April 30, 2007 as a special district subject to the provisions of this chapter but not subject to the provisions of
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-115(3): Nothing in this title may be construed to prohibit or limit a special district from providing on or after April 30, 2007 a service that it was authorized before that date to provide.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-116 Property exempt from taxation and execution.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
All property and assets of a special district are exempt from taxation and exempt from execution.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-117 Severability.
---------------------------------------------
A court's invalidation of any provision of this title may not be considered to affect the validity of any other provision of this title.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(1): "Applicable area" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(1)(a): for a county, the unincorporated area of the county that is included within the proposed special district; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(1)(b): for a municipality, the area of the municipality that is included within the proposed special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(2): "Governing body" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(2)(a): for a county or municipality, the legislative body of the county or municipality; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(2)(b): for a special district, the board of trustees of the special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-201(3): 17B-1-203(1)(c) "Groundwater right owner petition" means a petition under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206 Request certification -- Amended request.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1): 17B-1-204(2); 17B-1-205(1) Within 30 days after the filing of a request, the clerk of each county and the clerk or recorder of each municipality with which a request was filed shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1)(a): 17B-1-204(2); 17B-1-205(1) with the assistance of other county or municipal officers from whom the clerk or recorder requests assistance, determine, for the clerk or recorder's respective county or municipality, whether the request complies with the requirements of Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1)(b)(i): if the clerk or recorder determines that the request complies with the requirements:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1)(b)(i)(A): certify the request and deliver it to the legislative body of the county or municipality, as the case may be; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1)(b)(i)(B): mail or deliver written notification of the certification to the contact sponsor; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(1)(b)(ii): if the clerk or recorder determines that the request fails to comply with any of the applicable requirements, reject the request and notify the contact sponsor in writing of the rejection and the reasons for the rejection.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-206(3): Each county clerk or municipal clerk or recorder shall certify or reject requests in the order in which they are filed.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-207 Signature on request may be used on petition.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
A signature on a request may be used toward fulfilling the signature requirement of a petition:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-207(1): if the request notifies the signer in conspicuous language that the signature, unless withdrawn, would also be used for purposes of a petition to create a special district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-207(2): unless the signer files a written withdrawal of the signature before the petition is filed.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(2)(a)(ii): 17B-1-203(1)(d); (e) for a public hearing on a resolution, adoption of a resolution under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(2)(d)(i)(B): whether the service should be provided by the county or municipality or the proposed special district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(2)(d)(i)(C): all other matters relating to the request or the proposed special district; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(2)(d)(ii): for a public hearing on a resolution, allowing the public to ask questions of and obtain further information from the governing body holding the hearing regarding the issues contained in or raised by the resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(3): A quorum of each governing body holding a public hearing under this section shall be present throughout each hearing held by that governing body.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(4): Each hearing under this section shall be held on a weekday evening other than a holiday beginning no earlier than 6 p.m.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(5): At the beginning and end of each hearing concerning a resolution, the governing body shall announce the deadline for filing protests and generally explain the protest procedure and requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(6): (2)(c) Two or more county or municipal legislative bodies may jointly hold a hearing or set of hearings required under this section if all the requirements of this section, other than the requirements of Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-210(7)(b): the public hearing or set of public hearings is held as close to the applicable area as reasonably possible.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301 Board of trustees duties and powers.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(1)(a): Each special district shall be governed by a board of trustees which shall manage and conduct the business and affairs of the district and shall determine all questions of district policy.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(1)(b): All powers of a special district are exercised through the board of trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2): (3); (4) The board of trustees may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(a): fix the location of the special district's principal place of business and the location of all offices and departments, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(b): fix the times of meetings of the board of trustees;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(c): select and use an official district seal;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(d): (3); (4) subject to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(e): require district officers and employees charged with the handling of district funds to provide surety bonds in an amount set by the board or provide a blanket surety bond to cover officers and employees;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(f): contract for or employ professionals to perform work or services for the special district that cannot satisfactorily be performed by the officers or employees of the district;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(g): through counsel, prosecute on behalf of or defend the special district in all court actions or other proceedings in which the district is a party or is otherwise involved;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(h): adopt bylaws for the orderly functioning of the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(i): adopt and enforce rules and regulations for the orderly operation of the special district or for carrying out the district's purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(j): prescribe a system of civil service for district employees;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(k): on behalf of the special district, enter into contracts that the board considers to be for the benefit of the district;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(l): acquire, construct or cause to be constructed, operate, occupy, control, and use buildings, works, or other facilities for carrying out the purposes of the special district;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(m): on behalf of the special district, acquire, use, hold, manage, occupy, and possess property necessary to carry out the purposes of the district, dispose of property when the board considers it appropriate, and institute and maintain in the name of the district any action or proceeding to enforce, maintain, protect, or preserve rights or privileges associated with district property;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(n): delegate to a district officer the exercise of a district duty; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(2)(o): exercise all powers and perform all functions in the operation of the special district and its properties as are ordinarily exercised by the governing body of a political subdivision of the state and as are necessary to accomplish the purposes of the district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3): (3); 17B-1-304; (3)(b)(i); (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a): (3); 17B-1-304 As used in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a)(i): if any member of the special district board is elected, the period of time that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a)(i)(A): begins on the day on which an election is held to elect a special district board member; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a)(i)(B): ends on the day on which the special district board member-elect begins the member's term; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a)(ii): 17B-1-304 if any member of the special district board is appointed, the period of time that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a)(ii)(A): 17B-1-304 begins on the day on which an appointing authority posts a notice of vacancy in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(a)(ii)(B): ends on the day on which the person who is appointed by the special district board to fill the vacancy begins the person's term.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(b): (3)(b)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(b)(i): The special district may not hire during an interim vacancy period a manager, a chief executive officer, a chief administrative officer, an executive director, or a similar position to perform executive and administrative duties or functions.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(b)(ii): (3)(b)(i) Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(b)(ii)(A): the special district may hire an interim manager, a chief executive officer, a chief administrative officer, an executive director, or a similar position during an interim vacancy period; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(b)(ii)(B): the interim manager's, chief executive officer's, chief administrative officer's, or similar position's employment shall terminate once a new manager, chief executive officer, chief administrative officer, or similar position is hired by the new special district board after the interim vacancy period has ended.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(c): (3)(b) Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(c)(i): all the elected special district board members who held office on the day of the election for the special district board members, whose term of office was vacant for the election are re-elected to the special district board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(3)(c)(ii): all the appointed special district board members who were appointed whose term of appointment was expiring are re-appointed to the special district board.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-301(4): A special district board that hires an interim manager, a chief executive officer, a chief administrative officer, an executive director, or a similar position in accordance with this section may not, on or after May 10, 2011, enter into an employment contract that contains an automatic renewal provision with the interim manager, chief executive officer, chief administrative officer, executive director, or similar position.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304 Appointment procedures for appointed members -- Notice of vacancy.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(1): The appointing authority may, by resolution, appoint persons to serve as members of a special district board by following the procedures established by this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2): 63G-30-102
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2)(a): In any calendar year when appointment of a new special district board member is required, the appointing authority shall prepare a notice of vacancy that contains:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2)(a)(i): the positions that are vacant that shall be filled by appointment;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2)(a)(ii): the qualifications required to be appointed to those positions;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2)(a)(iii): the procedures for appointment that the governing body will follow in making those appointments; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2)(a)(iv): the person to be contacted and any deadlines that a person shall meet who wishes to be considered for appointment to those positions.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(2)(c): The appointing authority may bill the special district for the cost of preparing, printing, and publishing the notice.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(3)(b)(i): Title 52, Chapter 4, Open and Public Meetings Act comply with
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(3)(b)(ii): allow any interested persons to be heard; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(3)(b)(iii): adopt a resolution appointing a person to the special district board.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(3)(c): If no candidate for appointment to fill the vacancy receives a majority vote of the appointing authority, the appointing authority shall select the appointee from the two top candidates by lot.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-304(4): Persons appointed to serve as members of the special district board serve four-year terms, but may be removed for cause at any time after a hearing by two-thirds vote of the appointing body.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-305 Notice of offices to be filled.
---------------------------------------------------------------
On or before February 1 of each election year in which board members of a special district are elected, the board of each special district required to participate in an election that year shall prepare and transmit to the clerk of each county in which any part of the district is located a written notice that:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-305(1): designates the offices to be filled at that year's election; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-305(2): identifies the dates for filing a declaration of candidacy for those offices.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-309(2): Each officer serves at the pleasure of the board of trustees, but the board may designate a set term for officers.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311 Board member prohibited from district employment -- Exception.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(1): No elected or appointed member of the board of trustees of a special district may, while serving on the board, be employed by the district, whether as an employee or under a contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(2): No person employed by a special district, whether as an employee or under a contract, may serve on the board of that special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(3): (1); (2); 17B-1-307 A special district is not in violation of a prohibition described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(3)(a): treats a member of a board of trustees as an employee for income tax purposes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(3)(b): 17B-1-307 complies with the compensation limits of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(4): (1) This section does not apply to a special district if:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(4)(a): fewer than 3,000 people in the state live within 40 miles of the special district's boundaries or primary place of employment, measured over all weather public roads; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(4)(b): (1) with respect to the employment of a board of trustees member under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(4)(b)(i): the job opening has had reasonable public notice; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(4)(b)(ii): the person employed is the best qualified candidate for the position.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-311(5): Chapter 2a, Part 8, Public Transit District Act This section does not apply to a board of trustees of a large public transit district as described in

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-314 Compelling attendance at board meetings.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board of trustees of a special district may:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-314(1): compel the attendance of its own members at its meetings; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-314(2): provide penalties it considers necessary for the failure to attend.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-401 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-401(1): "Applicable area" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-401(1)(a): for a county, the unincorporated area of the county that is included within the area proposed for annexation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-401(1)(b): for a municipality, the area of the municipality that is included within the area proposed for annexation.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-401(2): "Retail" means, with respect to a service provided by a municipality or special district, that the service is provided directly to the ultimate user.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-401(3): "Wholesale" means, with respect to a service provided by a special district, that the service is not provided directly to the ultimate user but is provided to a retail provider.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402 Annexation of area outside  special district.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(1): An area outside the boundaries of a special district may be annexed to the special district, as provided in this part, in order to provide to the area a service that the special district provides.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(2): The area proposed to be annexed:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(2)(a): may consist of one or more noncontiguous areas; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(2)(b): need not be adjacent to the boundaries of the proposed annexing special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(3): 17B-1-214(3)(d) With respect to a special district in the creation of which an election was not required under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(3)(a): an unincorporated area of a county may not be annexed to the special district unless, after annexation, at least a majority of the unincorporated area of the county will be included in the special district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(3)(b): the annexation of any part of an area within a municipality shall include all of the area within the municipality.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-402(4): Title 63H, Chapter 1, Military Installation Development Authority Act A special district may not annex an area located within a project area described in a project area plan adopted by the military installation development authority under

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-403(1)(b): a resolution adopted by the legislative body of each county whose unincorporated area includes and each municipality whose boundaries include any of the area proposed to be annexed; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-403(1)(c): a resolution adopted by the board of trustees of the proposed annexing special district if, for at least 12 consecutive months immediately preceding adoption of the resolution, the special district has provided:

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-403(1)(c)(ii): a wholesale service to a provider of the same service that has provided that service on a retail basis to the area.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-418 Annexed area subject to fees and taxes.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
When an annexation under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-501 Definition.
-------------------------------------------
As used in this part, "receiving entity" means the entity that will, after the withdrawal of an area from a special district, provide to the withdrawn area the service that the special district previously provided to the area.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5 Feasibility study for a municipality's withdrawal from a special district providing fire protection, paramedic, and emergency services or law enforcement service -- Notice of hearing.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1): 17B-1-505(3)(a) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(a): "Feasibility consultant" means a person with expertise in:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(a)(i): the processes and economics of local government; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(a)(ii): the economics of providing fire protection, paramedic, and emergency services or law enforcement service.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(b): "Feasibility study" means a study to determine the functional and financial feasibility of a municipality's withdrawal from a first responder special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(c): "First responder district" means a special district, other than a municipal services district, that provides:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(c)(i): fire protection, paramedic, and emergency services; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(c)(ii): law enforcement service.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(1)(d): 17B-1-505(3)(a) "Withdrawing municipality" means a municipality whose legislative body has adopted a resolution under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(2)(c): 17B-1-505(6)(a) a feasibility study is a condition under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5): (6)(a); (6)(a); (6)(b) In conducting a feasibility study under this section, the feasibility consultant shall consider:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(a): population and population density within the withdrawing municipality;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(b): current and five-year projections of demographics and economic base in the withdrawing municipality, including household size and income, commercial and industrial development, and public facilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(c): projected growth in the withdrawing municipality during the next five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(d): (6)(a) subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(d)(i): the estimated cost if the first responder district continues to provide service; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(d)(ii): the estimated cost if the withdrawing municipality provides service;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(e): (6)(a) subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(e)(i): the municipality included in the first responder district's service area; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(e)(ii): the withdrawing municipality excluded from the first responder district's service area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(f): a projection of any new taxes per household that may be levied within the withdrawing municipality within five years after the withdrawal;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(g): the fiscal impact that the withdrawing municipality's withdrawal has on other municipalities and unincorporated areas served by the first responder district, including any rate increase that may become necessary to maintain required coverage ratios for the first responder district's debt;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(h): the physical and other assets that will be required by the withdrawing municipality to provide, without interruption or diminution of service, the same service that is being provided by the first responder district;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(i): the physical and other assets that will no longer be required by the first responder district to continue to provide the current level of service to the remainder of the first responder district, excluding the withdrawing municipality, and could be transferred to the withdrawing municipality;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(j): (6)(b) subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(k): a fair and equitable allocation of the debts, liabilities, and obligations of the first responder district and any local building authority of the first responder district, between the withdrawing municipality and the remaining first responder district, taking into consideration:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(k)(i): any requirement to maintain the excludability of interest from the income of the holder of the debt, liability, or obligation for federal income tax purposes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(k)(ii): any first responder district assets that have been purchased with the proceeds of bonds issued by the first responder district that the first responder district will retain and any of those assets that will be transferred to the withdrawing municipality;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(l): the number and classification of first responder district employees who will no longer be required to serve the remaining portions of the first responder district after the withdrawing municipality withdraws from the first responder district, including the dollar amount of the wages, salaries, and benefits attributable to the employees and the estimated cost associated with termination of the employees if the withdrawing municipality does not employ the employees;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(m): maintaining as a base, for a period of three years after withdrawal, the existing schedule of pay and benefits for first responder district employees who are transferred to the employment of the withdrawing municipality; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(5)(n): any other factor that the feasibility consultant considers relevant to the question of the withdrawing municipality's withdrawal from the first responder district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6): (5)(d); (e)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(a): (5)(d); (e) For purposes of Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(a)(i): the feasibility consultant shall assume a level and quality of service to be provided in the future to the withdrawing municipality that fairly and reasonably approximates the level and quality of service that the first responder district provides to the withdrawing municipality at the time of the feasibility study;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(a)(ii): in determining the present value cost of a service that the first responder district provides, the feasibility consultant shall consider:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(a)(ii)(A): the cost to the withdrawing municipality of providing the service for the first five years after the withdrawal; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(a)(ii)(B): the first responder district's present and five-year projected cost of providing the same service within the withdrawing municipality; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(a)(iii): the feasibility consultant shall consider inflation and anticipated growth in calculating the cost of providing service.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-505.5(6)(b): The feasibility consultant may not consider an allocation of first responder district assets or a transfer of first responder district employees to the extent that the allocation or transfer would impair the first responder district's ability to continue to provide the current level of service to the remainder of the first responder district without the withdrawing municipality, unless the first responder district consents to the allocation or transfer.

The itemized list of expenses may be submitted to the contact sponsor.  If the list of expenses is submitted to the contact sponsor within 21 days after receipt of the petition, the contact sponsor on behalf of the petitioners shall be required to pay the expenses to the special district within 90 days of receipt.  Until funds to cover the expenses are delivered to the special district, the district will have no obligation to proceed with the withdrawal and the time limits on the district stated in this part will be tolled. Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-509(1)(b): post notice of the public hearing and of the proposed withdrawal in at least four conspicuous places within the area proposed to be withdrawn, no less than five nor more than 30 days before the public hearing.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-509(2)(d): state that the petition or resolution may be examined during specified times and at a specified place in the special district; and

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-509(2)(e)(i): prior to the hearing, submit relevant comments and other information in writing to the board of trustees at a specified address in the special district; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-509(2)(e)(ii): at the hearing, present relevant comments and other information in writing and may also present comments and information orally.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(1): "Appropriation" means an allocation of money by the board of trustees for a specific purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(2): "Budget" means a plan of financial operations for a fiscal year which embodies estimates of proposed expenditures for given purposes and the proposed means of financing them, and may refer to the budget of a particular fund for which a budget is required by law or it may refer collectively to the budgets for all such funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(3): "Budget officer" means the person appointed by the special district board of trustees to prepare the budget for the district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(4): "Budget year" means the fiscal year for which a budget is prepared.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(5): 17B-1-602 "Calendar year entity" means a special district whose fiscal year begins January 1 and ends December 31 of each calendar year as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(6): "Current year" means the fiscal year in which a budget is prepared and adopted, which is the fiscal year next preceding the budget year.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(7): "Deficit" has the meaning given under generally accepted accounting principles as reflected in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(8): "Estimated revenue" means the amount of revenue estimated to be received from all sources during the budget year in each fund for which a budget is being prepared.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(9): 17B-1-642 "Financial officer" means the official under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(10): "Fiscal year" means the annual period for accounting for fiscal operations in each district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(11): 17B-1-602 "Fiscal year entity" means a special district whose fiscal year begins July 1 of each year and ends on June 30 of the following year as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(12): "Fund" has the meaning given under generally accepted accounting principles as reflected in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(13): "Fund balance" has the meaning given under generally accepted accounting principles as reflected in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(14): "General fund" is as defined by the Governmental Accounting Standards Board as reflected in the Uniform Accounting Manual for All Local Governments prepared by the Office of the Utah State Auditor.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(15): "Governmental funds" means the general fund, special revenue fund, debt service fund, and capital projects fund of a special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(16): "Interfund loan" means a loan of cash from one fund to another, subject to future repayment.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(17): "Last completed fiscal year" means the fiscal year next preceding the current fiscal year.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(18): "Proprietary funds" means enterprise funds and the internal service funds of a special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(19): "Public funds" means any money or payment collected or received by an officer or employee of a special district acting in an official capacity and includes money or payment to the officer or employee for services or goods provided by the district, or the officer or employee while acting within the scope of employment or duty.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(20): "Retained earnings" has the meaning given under generally accepted accounting principles as reflected in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(21): "Special district general fund" means the general fund used by a special district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-601(22): "Special fund" means any special district fund other than the special district's general fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-602 Fiscal year.
--------------------------------------------
The fiscal year of each special district shall be, as determined by the board of trustees:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-602(1): the calendar year; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-602(2): the period from July 1 to the following June 30.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-603 Uniform accounting system.
----------------------------------------------------------
The accounting records of each special district shall be established and maintained, and financial statements prepared from those records, in conformance with generally accepted accounting principles promulgated from time to time by authoritative bodies in the United States.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-604 Funds and account groups maintained.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Each district shall maintain, according to its own accounting needs, some or all of the funds and account groups in its system of accounts, as prescribed in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-606 Total of revenues to equal expenditures.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-606(1): 17B-1-605 The budget for each fund under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-606(2): Each budget shall specify in tabular form:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-606(2)(a): estimates of all anticipated revenues, classified by the account titles prescribed in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-606(2)(b): all appropriations for expenditures, classified by the account titles prescribed in the Uniform Accounting Manual for Special Districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-606(3): The total of the anticipated revenues shall equal the total of appropriated expenditures.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607 Tentative budget to be prepared -- Review by governing body.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(1): On or before the first regularly scheduled meeting of the board of trustees in November for a calendar year entity and May for a fiscal year entity, the budget officer of each special district shall prepare for the ensuing year, in a format prescribed by the state auditor, and file with the board of trustees a tentative budget for each fund for which a budget is required.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(2): (1)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(2)(a): (1) Each tentative budget under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(2)(a)(i): actual revenues and expenditures for the last completed fiscal year;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(2)(a)(ii): estimated total revenues and expenditures for the current fiscal year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(2)(a)(iii): the budget officer's estimates of revenues and expenditures for the budget year.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(2)(b): The budget officer shall estimate the amount of revenue available to serve the needs of each fund, estimate the portion to be derived from all sources other than general property taxes, and estimate the portion that shall be derived from general property taxes.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(3): The tentative budget, when filed by the budget officer with the board of trustees, shall contain the estimates of expenditures together with specific work programs and any other supporting data required by this part or requested by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(4): 17B-1-613 The board of trustees shall review, consider, and tentatively adopt the tentative budget in any regular meeting or special meeting called for that purpose and may amend or revise the tentative budget in any manner that the board considers advisable prior to public hearings, but no appropriation required for debt retirement and interest or reduction of any existing deficits under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(5)(b): substantially comply with all other provisions of this part with respect to notices and hearings; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-607(5)(c): pass the budget as soon after incorporation as feasible.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-610 Public hearing on tentatively adopted budget.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
At the time and place advertised, or at any time or any place to which the public hearing may be adjourned, the board of trustees shall:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-610(1): hold a public hearing on the budgets tentatively adopted; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-610(2): give all interested persons in attendance an opportunity to be heard on the estimates of revenues and expenditures or any item in the tentative budget of any fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611 Continuing authority of governing body.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
After the conclusion of the public hearing, the board of trustees:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611(1): may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611(1)(a): continue to review the tentative budget;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611(1)(b): insert any new items; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611(1)(c): increase or decrease items of expenditure that were the proper subject of consideration at the public hearing;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611(2): 17B-1-613 may not decrease the amount appropriated for debt retirement and interest or reduction of any existing deficits, as provided by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-611(3): shall increase or decrease the total anticipated revenue to equal the net change in proposed expenditures in the budget of each fund.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-613 Appropriations not to exceed estimated expendable revenue -- Appropriations for existing deficits.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-613(1): The board of trustees of a special district may not make any appropriation in the final budget of any fund in excess of the estimated expendable revenue for the budget year of the fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-613(2): If there is a deficit fund balance in a fund at the close of the last completed fiscal year, the board of trustees of a special district shall include an item of appropriation for the deficit in the current budget of the fund equal to:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-613(2)(a): at least 5% of the total revenue of the fund in the last completed fiscal year; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-613(2)(b): if the deficit is equal to less than 5% of the total revenue of the fund in the last completed fiscal year, the entire amount of the deficit.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-613(3): The provisions of this section do not require a special district to add revenue to a fund that is used for debt service of a limited obligation, unless the revenue is pledged toward the limited obligation.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-614 Adoption of final budget -- Certification and filing.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-614(1): 59-2-919; 59-2-923 The board of trustees of each special district shall by resolution adopt a budget for the ensuing fiscal year for each fund for which a budget is required under this part prior to the beginning of the fiscal year, except as provided in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-614(2): The special district's budget officer shall certify a copy of the final budget for each fund and file it with the state auditor within 30 days after adoption.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-615 Budgets in effect for budget year.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-615(1): Upon final adoption, each budget shall be in effect for the budget year, subject to amendment as provided in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-615(2): A certified copy of the adopted budgets shall be filed in the special district office and shall be available to the public during regular business hours.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-616 Property tax levy -- Amount in budget as basis for determining.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
From the effective date of the budget or of any amendment enacted prior to the date on which property taxes are levied, the amount stated as the amount of estimated revenue from property taxes shall constitute the basis for determining the property tax levy to be set by the board of trustees for the corresponding tax year, subject to the applicable limitations imposed by law.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-617 Fund expenditures -- Budget officer's duties.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-617(1): The budget officer of each special district shall require all expenditures within each fund to conform with the fund budget.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-617(2): 17B-1-623 No appropriation may be encumbered and no expenditure may be made against any fund appropriation unless there is sufficient unencumbered balance in the fund's appropriation, except in cases of emergency as provided in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-618 Purchasing procedures.
------------------------------------------------------
All purchases or encumbrances by a special district shall be made or incurred according to the purchasing procedures established for each district by the district's rulemaking authority, as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-619 Expenditures or encumbrances in excess of appropriations prohibited -- Processing claims.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-619(1): A special district may not make or incur expenditures or encumbrances in excess of total appropriations in the budget as adopted or as subsequently amended.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-619(2): An obligation contracted by any officer in excess of total appropriations in the budget is not enforceable against the district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-619(3): No check or warrant to cover a claim against an appropriation may be drawn until the claim has been processed as provided by this part.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-620 Transfer of appropriation balance between accounts in same fund.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-620(1): (2) The board of trustees of each special district shall establish policies for the transfer of any unencumbered or unexpended appropriation balance or portion of the balance from one account in a fund to another account within the same fund, subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-620(2): An appropriation for debt retirement and interest, reduction of deficit, or other appropriation required by law or covenant may not be reduced below the minimums required.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-621 Review of individual governmental fund budgets -- Hearing.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-621(1): The board of trustees of a special district may, at any time during the budget year, review the individual budgets of the governmental funds for the purpose of determining if the total of any of them should be increased.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-621(2): 17B-1-609; 17B-1-610 If the board of trustees decides that the budget total of one or more of these funds should be increased, it shall follow the procedures established in Sections


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-622 Amendment and increase of individual fund budgets.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-622(1): 17B-1-621 After holding the hearing referred to in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-622(2): 17B-1-605 The board of trustees may not adopt an amendment to the current year budgets of any of the funds established in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-623 Emergency expenditures.
-------------------------------------------------------
The board of trustees of a special district may, by resolution, amend a budget and authorize an expenditure of money that results in a deficit in the district's general fund balance if:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-623(1): the board determines that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-623(1)(a): an emergency exists; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-623(1)(b): the expenditure is reasonably necessary to meet the emergency; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-623(2): the expenditure is used to meet the emergency.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-624 Lapse of appropriations -- Exceptions.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
All unexpended or unencumbered appropriations, except capital projects fund appropriations, lapse at the end of the budget year to the respective fund balance.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-625 Transfer of balances in special funds.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
If the necessity for maintaining any special fund of a district ceases to exist and a balance remains in the fund, the board of trustees shall authorize the transfer of the balance to the fund balance in the general fund of the district, subject to the following:Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-625(1): 11-42-413; 11-42-701 Any balance remaining in a special assessment fund and not required in its guaranty fund shall be treated in the manner provided in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-625(2): Any balance remaining in a capital projects fund shall be transferred to the appropriate debt service fund or other fund as the bond covenants may require and otherwise to the fund balance account in the general fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-625(3): 17B-1-609; 17B-1-610 If any balance held in a trust fund for a specific purpose, other than a cemetery perpetual care trust fund, is to be transferred because its original purpose or restriction has ceased to exist, a public hearing shall be held in the manner provided in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-1-625(4): If the board of trustees decides, in conformity with applicable laws, that the need for continuing maintenance of its cemetery perpetual care trust fund no longer exists, it may transfer the balance in the fund to the capital projects fund for expenditure for land, buildings, and major improvements to be used exclusively for cemetery purposes.
