Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-907 Adding a new service within a service area.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
A service area may begin to provide within the boundaries of the service area a service that it had not previously provided by using the procedures set forth in

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1001 Title.
----------------------------------------
This part is known as the "Water Conservancy District Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002 Legislative intent -- Purpose of water conservancy districts.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1): It is the intent of the Legislature and the policy of the state to:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1)(a): provide for the conservation and development of the water and land resources of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1)(b): provide for the greatest beneficial use of water within the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1)(c): control and make use of all unappropriated waters in the state and to apply those waters to direct and supplemental beneficial uses including domestic, manufacturing, irrigation, and power;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1)(d): obtain from water in the state the highest duty for domestic uses and irrigation of lands in the state within the terms of applicable interstate compacts and other law;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1)(e): cooperate with the United States and its agencies under federal reclamation or other laws and to construct, finance, operate, and maintain works in the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(1)(f): promote the greater prosperity and general welfare of the people of the state by encouraging the organization of water conservancy districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2): (1) The creation and operation of water conservancy districts are a public use to help accomplish the intent and policy stated in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(a): be essentially for the benefit and advantage of the people of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(b): indirectly benefit all industries of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(c): indirectly benefit the state by increasing the value of taxable property in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(d): directly benefit municipalities by providing adequate supplies of water for domestic use;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(e): directly benefit lands to be irrigated or drained;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(f): directly benefit lands now under irrigation by stabilizing the flow of water in streams and by increasing flow and return flow of water to those streams; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1002(2)(g): promote the comfort, safety, and welfare of the people of the state.


Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003 Provisions applicable to water conservancy districts.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(1): Chapter 1, Provisions Applicable to All Special Districts Each water conservancy district is governed by and has the powers stated in:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(1)(a): this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(1)(b): Chapter 1, Provisions Applicable to All Special Districts
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(2): This part applies only to water conservancy districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(3): A water conservancy district is not subject to the provisions of any other part of this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(4): Chapter 1, Provisions Applicable to All Special Districts If there is a conflict between a provision in
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(5): Before September 30, 2019, a water conservancy district shall submit a written report to the Revenue and Taxation Interim Committee that describes, for the water conservancy district's fiscal year that ended in 2018, the percentage and amount of revenue in the water conservancy district from:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(5)(a): property taxes;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(5)(b): water rates; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1003(5)(c): all other sources.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007 Contract assessments -- Notice.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1): 17D-1-301; 17D-1-301; (3); (3) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(a): "Assessed land" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(a)(i): for a contract assessment under a water contract with a private water user, the land owned by the private water user that receives the beneficial use of water under the water contract; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(a)(ii): for a contract assessment under a water contract with a public water user, the land within the boundaries of the public water user that is within the boundaries of the water conservancy district and that receives the beneficial use of water under the water contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(b): "Contract assessment" means an assessment levied as provided in this section by a water conservancy district on assessed land.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(c): 17D-1-301; 17D-1-301 "Governing body" means:

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(h)(ii): that enters into a water contract with the district.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(i): "Water contract" means a contract between a water conservancy district and a private water user or a public water user under which the water user purchases, leases, or otherwise acquires the beneficial use of water from the water conservancy district for the benefit of:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1007(1)(i)(i): land owned by the private water user; or

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1008 Subdistricts to become water conservancy districts.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Each water conservancy subdistrict, created and operating under the law in effect before April 30, 2007 and existing on April 30, 2007, shall, on that date, become a water conservancy district.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1105 Creation of municipal services district.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1105(1): Notwithstanding any other provision of law, the process to create a municipal services district is initiated by a resolution proposing the creation of the municipal services district, adopted by the legislative body of the county whose unincorporated area includes any of the proposed municipal services district.

Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107 Exclusion of rural real property.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(1): As used in this section, "rural real property" means an area:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(1)(a): zoned primarily for manufacturing, commercial, or agricultural purposes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(1)(b): that does not include residential units with a density greater than one unit per acre.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2): 17-41-101 Unless an owner gives written consent, rural real property may not be included in a municipal services district if the rural real property:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(a): consists of 1,500 or more contiguous acres of rural real property consisting of one or more tax parcels;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(b): is not contiguous to but is used in connection with rural real property that consists of 1,500 acres or more contiguous acres of real property consisting of one or more tax parcels;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(c): is owned, managed, or controlled by a person, company, or association, including a parent, subsidiary, or affiliate related to the owner of 1,500 or more contiguous acres of rural real property consisting of one or more tax parcels; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(d): 17-41-101 is located in whole or in part in one of the following as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(d)(i): an agricultural protection area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(d)(ii): a mining protection area; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(2)(d)(iii): an industrial protection area.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3): (3)(b); (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(a): (3)(b) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(b): An owner may withdraw consent by submitting a written and signed request to the municipal services district board of trustees that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(b)(i): identifies and describes the rural real property to be withdrawn; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(b)(ii): requests that the rural real property be withdrawn.
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(c): (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(c)(i): (3)(b) No later than 30 days after the day on which the municipal services district board of trustees receives a request that complies with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17B-2a-1107(3)(c)(ii): The rural real property is withdrawn from and no longer in the jurisdiction of the municipal services district upon adoption of the resolution.
